The day covers a range of tried and tested techniques that create the right environment for good things to happen.\nKey topics covered in day three include:\n\nCollaboration and co-design\nStakeholder engagement\nDesign walls and showcases\u00a0\nConcept elaboration\nCollaborative prioritisisation\nCommunicating the future vision using journey maps\n\nWho is it for\nThese workshops are ideal for anyone tasked with helping their organisation become more customer-centred.
